 [10\*\*\*](10000.md) | [11\*\*\*](11000.md) | [12\*\*\*](12000.md) | [13\*\*\*](13000.md) | [14\*\*\*](14000.md) | [15\*\*\*](15000.md) | [16\*\*\*](16000.md) | [17\*\*\*](17000.md) | [18\*\*\*](18000.md) | [19\*\*\*](19000.md) | [1A\*\*\*](1A000.md) | [1B\*\*\*](1B000.md) | [1C\*\*\*](1C000.md) | [1D\*\*\*](1D000.md) | [1E\*\*\*](1E000.md) | [1F\*\*\*](1F000.md) |

--------------------

`code`: as code span, &nbsp; **none**: character only, &nbsp; **txt**: character + VS15(U+FE0E), &nbsp; **emo**: character + VS16(U+FE0F)

| U+ |  0<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | 1<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | 2<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | 3<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | 4<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | 5<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | 6<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | 7<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | 8<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | 9<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | A<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | B<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | C<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | D<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | E<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo | F<br>`code`<br>none<br>txt<br>emo |
